Filters may modify headers and cause a new route to be selected, by asking HCM to\n443: clear the route cache and requesting HCM to reevaluate the route selection. onStreamComplete()\\n- `StreamDecoderFilter` - Interface for filters processing request data (headers, data, trailers) with methods like decodeHeaders(), decodeData(), decodeTrailers()\\n- `StreamEncoderFilter` - Interface for filters processing response data (headers, data, trailers) with methods like encodeHeaders(), encodeData(), encodeTrailers()\\n- `StreamFilter` - Combines both decoder and encoder interfaces\\n- Return status enums: `FilterHeadersStatus`, `FilterDataStatus`, `FilterTrailersStatus` control filter chain iteration\\n\\n## Filter Chain Manager and Factory Interfaces (envoy/http/filter_factory.h)\\nThese interfaces define the contract for filter chain creation:\\n- `FilterChainFactory` - Called when a new HTTP stream is created to instantiate the filter chain\\n- `FilterChainManager` - Acts as the \\\"sink\\\" that receives filter factories and builds the filter chain\\n- `FilterChainFactoryCallbacks` - Provides methods like addStreamDecoderFilter(), addStreamEncoderFilter(), addAccessLogHandler() to register filters with the chain\\n- `FilterFactoryCb` - Typedef for the factory callback function that creates and registers filter instances\\n- `FilterContext` - Contextual information about the filter (config name, filter name)\\n- `FilterChainOptions` - Options for customizing filter chain creation\\n\\n## Filter Factory Registry (envoy/server/filter_config.h)\\nThe registration system:\\n- `NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory` - Base interface for HTTP filter factories registered by name\\n- `UpstreamHttpFilterConfigFactory` - Base interface for upstream HTTP filters\\n- These implement the Registry pattern allowing filter configurations to be looked up and instantiated\\n\\n## Per-Request Filter Chain Execution (source/common/http/filter_manager.h, filter_manager.cc)\\nThe core execution engine:\\n- `FilterManager` - Manages execution of the filter chain for a single request/response stream, implementing both decoder and encoder phases\\n- `DownstreamFilterManager` - Specialized FilterManager for downstream requests\\n- `ActiveStreamFilterBase` - Base for active filter wrappers that handle filter callbacks and state transitions\\n- `ActiveStreamDecoderFilter` - Wraps a decoder filter and manages its execution during decode phase\\n- `ActiveStreamEncoderFilter` - Wraps an encoder filter and manages its execution during encode phase\\n- The FilterManager iterates through decoder filters in sequence during request processing and encoder filters in reverse sequence during response processing\\n- Key methods: `decodeHeaders()`, `encodeHeaders()`, `decodeData()`, `encodeData()`, `decodeTrailers()`, `encodeTrailers()`\\n\\n## HTTP Connection Manager (source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h, conn_manager_impl.cc)\\nThe main HTTP protocol handler:\\n- `ConnectionManagerImpl` - Network filter that manages HTTP connections and creates per-stream FilterManagers\\n- Creates a new FilterManager for each HTTP stream\\n- Calls the FilterChainFactory when a new stream arrives to build the filter chain\\n\\n## Filter Chain Creation Flow (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h, filter_chain_helper.cc, source/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/config.h, config.cc)\\nThe process of instantiating filter chains:\\n- `HttpConnectionManagerConfig` - Configuration object that implements FilterChainFactory interface\\n- `FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories()` - Static utility that applies filter factories to the FilterChainManager\\n- `FilterChainHelper` - Template class that manages the complete filter chain creation process including dynamic filter loading\\n- When a new stream arrives, HttpConnectionManagerConfig::createFilterChain() is called\\n- This calls FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories() which applies each configured filter factory in order\\n- Each factory callback is applied via FilterChainManager::applyFilterFactoryCb()\\n\\n## Filter Factory Base Classes (source/extensions/filters/http/common/factory_base.h)\\nReusable implementations for filter factories:\\n- `FactoryBase<ConfigProto, RouteSpecificConfigProto>` - Template base for downstream-only filters\\n- `DualFactoryBase<ConfigProto, RouteSpecificConfigProto>` - Template base for filters supporting both upstream and downstream contexts\\n- Provides default implementations of createFilterFactoryFromProto() methods\\n\\n## Dynamic Filter Configuration (source/common/filter/config_discovery_impl.h)\\nSupport for dynamic filter configuration:\\n- `HttpDynamicFilterConfigProviderImpl` - Allows filter configuration to be updated at runtime via xDS without restarting\\n- Manages subscription to filter config updates\\n\\n## Helper Utilities (source/extensions/filters/http/common/pass_through_filter.h)\\n- `PassThroughFilter` - Convenient base class for filters that don't modify the stream data\\n- Provides default implementations of all filter methods that just continue the chain\\n\\nThis architecture enables Envoy's flexible HTTP filter extensibility where filters can be plugged in at configuration time, dynamically loaded via xDS, and executed in sequence with control over iteration flow based on status Interfaces (envoy/http/filter.h)\\nThe foundation consists of filter interface classes:\\n- `StreamFilterBase` - Base interface for all filters with lifecycle methods like onDestroy() and onStreamComplete()\\n- `StreamDecoderFilter` - Interface for filters processing request data (headers, data, trailers) with methods like decodeHeaders(), decodeData(), decodeTrailers()\\n- `StreamEncoderFilter` - Interface for filters processing response data (headers, data, trailers) with methods like encodeHeaders(), encodeData(), encodeTrailers()\\n- `StreamFilter` - Combines both decoder and encoder interfaces\\n- Return status enums: `FilterHeadersStatus`, `FilterDataStatus`, `FilterTrailersStatus` control filter chain iteration\\n\\n## Filter Chain Manager and Factory Interfaces (envoy/http/filter_factory.h)\\nThese interfaces define the contract for filter chain creation:\\n- `FilterChainFactory` - Called when a new HTTP stream is created to instantiate the filter chain\\n- `FilterChainManager` - Acts as the \\\"sink\\\" that receives filter factories and builds the filter chain\\n- `FilterChainFactoryCallbacks` - Provides methods like addStreamDecoderFilter(), addStreamEncoderFilter(), addAccessLogHandler() to register filters with the chain\\n- `FilterFactoryCb` - Typedef for the factory callback function that creates and registers filter instances\\n- `FilterContext` - Contextual information about the filter (config name, filter name)\\n- `FilterChainOptions` - Options for customizing filter chain creation\\n\\n## Filter Factory Registry (envoy/server/filter_config.h)\\nThe registration system:\\n- `NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory` - Base interface for HTTP filter factories registered by name\\n- `UpstreamHttpFilterConfigFactory` - Base interface for upstream HTTP filters\\n- These implement the Registry pattern allowing filter configurations to be looked up and instantiated\\n\\n## Per-Request Filter Chain Execution (source/common/http/filter_manager.h, filter_manager.cc)\\nThe core execution engine:\\n- `FilterManager` - Manages execution of the filter chain for a single request/response stream, implementing both decoder and encoder phases\\n- `DownstreamFilterManager` - Specialized FilterManager for downstream requests\\n- `ActiveStreamFilterBase` - Base for active filter wrappers that handle filter callbacks and state transitions\\n- `ActiveStreamDecoderFilter` - Wraps a decoder filter and manages its execution during decode phase\\n- `ActiveStreamEncoderFilter` - Wraps an encoder filter and manages its execution during encode phase\\n- The FilterManager iterates through decoder filters in sequence during request processing and encoder filters in reverse sequence during response processing\\n- Key methods: `decodeHeaders()`, `encodeHeaders()`, `decodeData()`, `encodeData()`, `decodeTrailers()`, `encodeTrailers()`\\n\\n## HTTP Connection Manager (source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h, conn_manager_impl.cc)\\nThe main HTTP protocol handler:\\n- `ConnectionManagerImpl` - Network filter that manages HTTP connections and creates per-stream FilterManagers\\n- Creates a new FilterManager for each HTTP stream\\n- Calls the FilterChainFactory when a new stream arrives to build the filter chain\\n\\n## Filter Chain Creation Flow (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h, filter_chain_helper.cc, source/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/config.h, config.cc)\\nThe process of instantiating filter chains:\\n- `HttpConnectionManagerConfig` - Configuration object that implements FilterChainFactory interface\\n- `FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories()` - Static utility that applies filter factories to the FilterChainManager\\n- `FilterChainHelper` - Template class that manages the complete filter chain creation process including dynamic filter loading\\n- When a new stream arrives, HttpConnectionManagerConfig::createFilterChain() is called\\n- This calls FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories() which applies each configured filter factory in order\\n- Each factory callback is applied via FilterChainManager::applyFilterFactoryCb()\\n\\n## Filter Factory Base Classes (source/extensions/filters/http/common/factory_base.h)\\nReusable implementations for filter factories:\\n- `FactoryBase<ConfigProto, RouteSpecificConfigProto>` - Template base for downstream-only filters\\n- `DualFactoryBase<ConfigProto, RouteSpecificConfigProto>` - Template base for filters supporting both upstream and downstream contexts\\n- Provides default implementations of createFilterFactoryFromProto() methods\\n\\n## Dynamic Filter Configuration (source/common/filter/config_discovery_impl.h)\\nSupport for dynamic filter configuration:\\n- `HttpDynamicFilterConfigProviderImpl` - Allows filter configuration to be updated at runtime via xDS without restarting\\n- Manages subscription to filter config updates\\n\\n## Helper Utilities (source/extensions/filters/http/common/pass_through_filter.h)\\n- `PassThroughFilter` - Convenient base class for filters that don't modify the stream data\\n- Provides default implementations of all filter methods that just continue the chain\\n\\nThis architecture enables Envoy's flexible HTTP filter extensibility where filters can be plugged in at configuration time, dynamically loaded via xDS, and executed in sequence with control over iteration flow based on status returns.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
